### <a name="34-main-and-backup-boot-checksum-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-737">3.4 Subrecciones de suma de comprobación principal y de arranque de copia de seguridad</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-737">3.4 Main and Backup Boot Checksum Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-738">Las sumas de comprobación principal y de arranque de copia de seguridad contienen cada una un patrón de repetición de la suma de comprobación de cuatro bytes del contenido de todas las demás subrecciones en sus respectivas regiones de arranque.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-738">The Main and Backup Boot Checksums each contain a repeating pattern of the four-byte checksum of the contents of all other sub-regions in their respective Boot regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-739">El cálculo de suma de comprobación no debe incluir los campos VolumeFlags y PercentInUse en sus respectivos sectores de arranque (consulte [la figura 1).](#figure-1-boot-checksum-computation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-739">The checksum calculation shall not include the VolumeFlags and PercentInUse fields in their respective Boot Sector (see [Figure 1](#figure-1-boot-checksum-computation)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-740">El patrón de repetición de la suma de comprobación de cuatro bytes rellena su subrecciones de suma de comprobación de arranque correspondientes desde el principio hasta el final de la subrecciones.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-740">The repeating pattern of the four-byte checksum fills its respective Boot Checksum sub-region from the beginning to the end of the sub-region.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-741">Antes de usar el contenido de cualquiera de las otras regiones en las regiones Main o Backup Boot, las implementaciones deben comprobar su contenido validando su respectiva suma de comprobación de arranque.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-741">Prior to using the contents of any of the other sub-regions in either the Main or Backup Boot regions, implementations shall verify their contents by validating their respective Boot Checksum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-742">Aunque la operación de formato inicial rellenará las sumas de comprobación principal y de arranque de copia de seguridad con el patrón de suma de comprobación que se repite, las implementaciones actualizarán estos sectores a medida que cambie el contenido de los otros sectores de sus respectivas regiones de arranque.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-742">While the initial format operation will populate both the Main and Backup Boot Checksums with the repeating checksum pattern, implementations shall update these sectors as the contents of the other sectors in their respective Boot regions change.</span></span>

<div id="figure-1-boot-checksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-743">**Figura 1 Cálculo de suma de comprobación de arranque**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-743">**Figure 1 Boot Checksum Computation**</span></span>

```c
UInt32 BootChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Sectors,        // points to an in-memory copy of the 11 sectors
    USHORT   BytesPerSector
)
{
    UInt32 NumberOfBytes = (UInt32)BytesPerSector * 11;
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt32 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        if ((Index == 106) || (Index == 107) || (Index == 112))
        {
            continue;
        }
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Sectors[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

## <a name="4-file-allocation-table-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-744">4 Región de tabla de asignación de archivos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-744">4 File Allocation Table Region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-745">La región De tabla de asignación de archivos (FAT) puede contener hasta dos FAT, una en la subr regiones First FAT y otra en la segunda subr region fat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-745">The File Allocation Table (FAT) region may contain up to two FATs, one in the First FAT sub-region and another in the Second FAT sub-region.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-746">El campo NumberOfLats describe el número de FAT que contiene esta región.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-746">The NumberOfFats field describes how many FATs this region contains.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-747">Los valores válidos para el campo NumberOfPlants son 1 y 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-747">The valid values for the NumberOfFats field are 1 and 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-748">Por lo tanto, la primera sub-región FAT siempre contiene un FAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-748">Therefore, the First FAT sub-region always contains a FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-749">Si el campo NumberOfAturas es dos, la segunda subrecciones FAT también contiene una fat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-749">If the NumberOfFats field is two, then the Second FAT sub-region also contains a FAT.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-750">El campo ActiveAtura del campo VolumeFlags describe qué FAT está activo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-750">The ActiveFat field of the VolumeFlags field describes which FAT is active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-751">Solo el campo VolumeFlags del sector de arranque principal está actual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-751">Only the VolumeFlags field in the Main Boot Sector is current.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-752">Las implementaciones deben tratar el FAT que no está activo como obsoleto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-752">Implementations shall treat the FAT which is not active as stale.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-753">El uso de FAT inactivo y el cambio entre las FAT son específicos de la implementación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-753">Use of the inactive FAT and switching between FATs is implementation specific.</span></span>

### <a name="41-first-and-second-fat-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-754">4.1 Subrecciones FAT de primera y segunda</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-754">4.1 First and Second FAT Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-755">Una FAT describirá las cadenas de clúster en el montón de clúster (consulte [la tabla 11).](#table-11-file-allocation-table-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-755">A FAT shall describe cluster chains in the Cluster Heap (see [Table 11](#table-11-file-allocation-table-structure)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-756">Una cadena de clústeres es una serie de clústeres que proporciona espacio para registrar el contenido de archivos, directorios y otras estructuras del sistema de archivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-756">A cluster chain is a series of clusters which provides space for recording the contents of files, directories, and other file system structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-757">FAT representa una cadena de clúster como una lista de índices de clúster vinculadas de forma singly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-757">A FAT represents a cluster chain as a singly-linked list of cluster indices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-758">A excepción de las dos primeras entradas, cada entrada de fat representa exactamente un clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-758">With the exception of the first two entries, every entry in a FAT represents exactly one cluster.</span></span>

#### <a name="411-fatentry0-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-801">4.1.1 Campo FatEntry \[ 0 \]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-801">4.1.1 FatEntry\[0\] Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-802">El campo FatEntry 0 describirá el tipo de medio en el primer byte (el byte de orden más bajo) y contendrá FFh en los \[ \] tres bytes restantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-802">The FatEntry\[0\] field shall describe the media type in the first byte (the lowest order byte) and shall contain FFh in the remaining three bytes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-803">El tipo de medio (el primer byte) debe ser F8h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-803">The media type (the first byte) should be F8h.</span></span>

#### <a name="412-fatentry1-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-804">4.1.2 Campo FatEntry \[ 1 \]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-804">4.1.2 FatEntry\[1\] Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-805">El campo FatEntry \[ 1 \] solo existe debido a la precedencia histórica y no describe nada de interés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-805">The FatEntry\[1\] field only exists due to historical precedence and does not describe anything of interest.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-806">El valor válido para este campo es FFFFFFFFh.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-806">The valid value for this field is FFFFFFFFh.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-807">Las implementaciones inicializarán este campo en su valor prescrito y no deben usar este campo para ningún propósito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-807">Implementations shall initialize this field to its prescribed value and should not use this field for any purpose.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-808">Las implementaciones no deben interpretar este campo y deben conservar su contenido en todas las operaciones que modifican los campos circundantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-808">Implementations should not interpret this field and shall preserve its contents across operations which modify surrounding fields.</span></span>

#### <a name="413-fatentry2--fatentryclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-809">4.1.3 FatEntry \[ 2 \] ... Campos FatEntry \[ ClusterCount+1 \]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-809">4.1.3 FatEntry\[2\] ... FatEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-810">Cada campo FatEntry de esta matriz debe representar un clúster en el montón de clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-810">Each FatEntry field in this array shall represent a cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-811">FatEntry 2 representa el primer clúster del montón de clúster y \[ \] FatEntry \[ ClusterCount+1 representa el último \] clúster del montón de clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-811">FatEntry\[2\] represents the first cluster in the Cluster Heap and FatEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] represents the last cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-812">El intervalo válido de valores para estos campos debe ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-812">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-813">Entre 2 y ClusterCount + 1, ambos incluidos, que apuntan al siguiente FatEntry en la cadena de clúster dada; el fatEntry dado no debe apuntar a ninguna FatEntry que le preceda en la cadena de clúster determinada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-813">Between 2 and ClusterCount + 1, inclusively, which points to the next FatEntry in the given cluster chain; the given FatEntry shall not point to any FatEntry which precedes it in the given cluster chain</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-814">Exactamente FFFFFFF7h, que marca el clúster correspondiente de FatEntry dado como "malo"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-814">Exactly FFFFFFF7h, which marks the given FatEntry's corresponding cluster as "bad"</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-815">Exactamente FFFFFFFFh, que marca el clúster correspondiente de FatEntry dado como el último clúster de una cadena de clúster; este es el único valor válido para el último FatEntry de cualquier cadena de clúster determinada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-815">Exactly FFFFFFFFh, which marks the given FatEntry's corresponding cluster as the last cluster of a cluster chain; this is the only valid value for the last FatEntry of any given cluster chain</span></span>

## <a name="5-data-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-816">5 Región de datos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-816">5 Data Region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-817">La región Datos contiene el montón de clúster, que proporciona espacio administrado para estructuras, directorios y archivos del sistema de archivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-817">The Data region contains the Cluster Heap, which provides managed space for file system structures, directories, and files.</span></span>

### <a name="51-cluster-heap-sub-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-818">5.1 Subr regiones del montón de clúster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-818">5.1 Cluster Heap Sub-region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-819">La estructura del montón de clúster es muy sencilla (vea [la tabla 12](#table-12-cluster-heap-structure)); cada serie consecutiva de sectores describe un clúster, como define el campo SectorsPerClusterShift.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-819">The Cluster Heap's structure is very simple (see [Table 12](#table-12-cluster-heap-structure)); each consecutive series of sectors describes one cluster, as the SectorsPerClusterShift field defines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-820">Lo importante es que el primer clúster del montón de clústeres tiene el índice dos, que corresponde directamente al índice de FatEntry \[ \] 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-820">Importantly, the first cluster of the Cluster Heap has index two, which directly corresponds to the index of FatEntry\[2\].</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-821">En un volumen ex RAID, un mapa de bits de asignación (consulte la sección [7.1.5)](#715-allocation-bitmap)mantiene el registro del estado de asignación de todos los clústeres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-821">In an exFAT volume, an Allocation Bitmap (see [Section 7.1.5](#715-allocation-bitmap)) maintains the record of the allocation state of all clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-822">Se trata de una diferencia significativa con respecto a los predecesores de exAPI (FAT12, FAT16 y FAT32), en los que fat mantiene un registro del estado de asignación de todos los clústeres del montón de clústeres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-822">This is a significant difference from exFAT's predecessors (FAT12, FAT16, and FAT32), in which a FAT maintained a record of the allocation state of all clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<td><span data-ttu-id="a54af-847">Cluster[ClusterCount+1]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-847">Cluster[ClusterCount+1]</span></span></td>

#### <a name="511-cluster2--clusterclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-852">5.1.1 Clúster \[ 2 \] ... Cluster \[ ClusterCount+1 \] Campos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-852">5.1.1 Cluster\[2\] ... Cluster\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-853">Cada campo Cluster de esta matriz es una serie de sectores contiguos, cuyo tamaño se define mediante el campo SectorsPerClusterShift.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-853">Each Cluster field in this array is a series of contiguous sectors, whose size is defined by the SectorsPerClusterShift field.</span></span>

## <a name="6-directory-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-854">6 Estructura de directorios</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-854">6 Directory Structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-855">El sistema de archivos exSTRUCCIONES usa un enfoque de árbol de directorios para administrar las estructuras del sistema de archivos y los archivos que existen en el montón de clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-855">The exFAT file system uses a directory tree approach to manage the file system structures and files which exist in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-856">Los directorios tienen una relación uno a varios entre el elemento primario y el secundario en el árbol de directorios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-856">Directories have a one-to-many relationship between parent and child in the directory tree.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-857">El directorio al que hace referencia el campo FirstClusterOfRootDirectory es la raíz del árbol de directorios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-857">The directory to which the FirstClusterOfRootDirectory field refers is the root of the directory tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-858">Todos los demás directorios descienden del directorio raíz de forma vinculada de forma singly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-858">All other directories descend from the root directory in a singly-linked fashion.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-859">Cada directorio consta de una serie de entradas de directorio (vea [la tabla 13).](#table-13-directory-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-859">Each directory consists of a series of directory entries (see [Table 13](#table-13-directory-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-860">Una o varias entradas de directorio se combinan en un conjunto de entradas de directorio que describe algo de interés, como una estructura del sistema de archivos, un directorio o un archivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-860">One or more directory entries combine into a directory entry set which describes something of interest, such as a file system structure, sub-directory, or file.</span></span>

### <a name="62-generic-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-891">6.2 Plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-891">6.2 Generic DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-892">La plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry proporciona la definición base para las entradas de directorio (vea [la tabla 14).](#table-14-generic-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-892">The Generic DirectoryEntry template provides the base definition for directory entries (see [Table 14](#table-14-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-893">Todas las estructuras de entrada de directorio derivan de esta plantilla y solo las estructuras de entrada de directorio definidas por Microsoft son válidas (ex LDAP no tiene aprovisionamientos para las estructuras de entrada de directorio definidas por el fabricante, excepto como se define en la sección [7.8](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry) y [la sección 7.9).](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-893">All directory entry structures derive from this template and only Microsoft-defined directory entry structures are valid (exFAT does not have provisions for manufacturer-defined directory entry structures except as defined in [Section 7.8](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.9](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-894">La capacidad de interpretar la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry es obligatoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-894">The ability to interpret the Generic DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

#### <a name="621-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-918">6.2.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-918">6.2.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-919">El campo EntryType tiene tres modos de uso que define el valor del campo (vea la lista siguiente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-919">The EntryType field has three modes of usage which the value of the field defines (see list below).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-920">00h, que es un marcador de fin de directorio y se aplican las condiciones siguientes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-920">00h, which is an end-of-directory marker and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-921">Todos los demás campos del DirectoryEntry especificado están reservados realmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-921">All other fields in the given DirectoryEntry are actually reserved</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-922">Todas las entradas de directorio subsiguientes del directorio especificado también son marcadores de fin de directorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-922">All subsequent directory entries in the given directory also are end-of-directory markers</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-923">Los marcadores de fin de directorio solo son válidos fuera de los conjuntos de entrada de directorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-923">End-of-directory markers are only valid outside directory entry sets</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-924">Las implementaciones pueden sobrescribir los marcadores de fin de directorio según sea necesario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-924">Implementations may overwrite end-of-directory markers as necessary</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-925">Entre 01h y 7Fh inclusive, que es un marcador de entrada de directorio sin usar y se aplican las condiciones siguientes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-925">Between 01h and 7Fh inclusively, which is an unused-directory-entry marker and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-926">Todos los demás campos del DirectoryEntry especificado no están definidos realmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-926">All other fields in the given DirectoryEntry are actually undefined</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-927">Las entradas de directorio no utilizadas solo son válidas fuera de los conjuntos de entrada de directorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-927">Unused directory entries are only valid outside of directory entry sets</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-928">Las implementaciones pueden sobrescribir las entradas de directorio no utilizadas según sea necesario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-928">Implementations may overwrite unused directory entries as necessary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-929">Este intervalo de valores corresponde al campo InUse (consulte la sección [6.2.1.4)](#6214-inuse-field)que contiene el valor 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-929">This range of values corresponds to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) containing the value 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-930">Entre 81 h y FFh inclusive, que es una entrada de directorio normal y se aplican las condiciones siguientes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-930">Between 81h and FFh inclusively, which is a regular directory entry and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-931">El contenido del campo EntryType (consulte [la tabla 15)](#table-15-generic-entrytype-field-structure)determina el diseño del resto de la estructura DirectoryEntry.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-931">The contents of the EntryType field (see [Table 15](#table-15-generic-entrytype-field-structure)) determine the layout of the remainder of the DirectoryEntry structure</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-932">Este intervalo de valores, y solo este intervalo de valores, son válidos dentro de un conjunto de entradas de directorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-932">This range of values, and only this range of values, are valid inside a directory entry set</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-933">Este intervalo de valores corresponde directamente al campo InUse (consulte la sección [6.2.1.4)](#6214-inuse-field)que contiene el valor 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-933">This range of values directly corresponds to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) containing the value 1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-934">Para evitar modificaciones en el campo InUse (consulte la sección [6.2.1.4)](#6214-inuse-field)que da lugar erróneamente a un marcador de fin de directorio, el valor 80h no es válido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-934">To prevent modifications to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) erroneously resulting in an end-of-directory marker, the value 80h is invalid.</span></span>

<th><span data-ttu-id="a54af-936"><strong>Nombre del campo</strong></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-936"><strong>Field Name</strong></span></span></th>
<th><p><span data-ttu-id="a54af-937"><strong>Offset</strong></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-937"><strong>Offset</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span data-ttu-id="a54af-938"><strong>(bit)</strong></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-938"><strong>(bit)</strong></span></span></p></th>

##### <a name="6211-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-958">6.2.1.1 Campo TypeCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-958">6.2.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-959">El campo TypeCode describe parcialmente el tipo específico de la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-959">The TypeCode field partially describes the specific type of the given directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-960">Este campo, además de los campos TypeImportance y TypeCategory (vea sección [6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field) y sección [6.2.1.3,](#6213-typecategory-field)respectivamente), identifica de forma única el tipo de la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-960">This field, plus the TypeImportance and TypeCategory fields (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field) and [Section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field), respectively) uniquely identify the type of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-961">Todos los valores posibles de este campo son válidos, a menos que los campos TypeImportance y TypeCategory contengan el valor 0; En ese caso, el valor 0 no es válido para este campo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-961">All possible values of this field are valid, unless the TypeImportance and TypeCategory fields both contain the value 0; in that case, the value 0 is invalid for this field.</span></span>

##### <a name="6212-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-962">6.2.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-962">6.2.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-963">El campo TypeImportance describirá la importancia de la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-963">The TypeImportance field shall describe the importance of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-964">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-964">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-965">0, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio dada es crítica (consulte la [sección 6.3.1.2.1](#63121-critical-primary-directory-entries) y la sección [6.4.1.2.1](#64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries) para las entradas de directorio principal y secundaria críticas, respectivamente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-965">0, which means the given directory entry is critical (see [Section    6.3.1.2.1](#63121-critical-primary-directory-entries) and [Section 6.4.1.2.1](#64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries) for critical primary and critical secondary   directory entries, respectively)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-966">1, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio dada es benigna (consulte la sección [6.3.1.2.2](#63122-benign-primary-directory-entries) y la [sección 6.4.1.2.2 para](#64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries) las entradas benignas de directorio principal e secundario benigno, respectivamente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-966">1, which means the given directory entry is benign (see [Section    6.3.1.2.2](#63122-benign-primary-directory-entries) and [Section 6.4.1.2.2](#64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries) for benign primary and benign secondary   directory entries, respectively)</span></span>

##### <a name="6213-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-967">6.2.1.3 Campo TypeCategory</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-967">6.2.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-968">El campo TypeCategory describirá la categoría de la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-968">The TypeCategory field shall describe the category of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-969">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-969">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-970">0, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio determinada es principal (consulte [la sección 6.3)](#63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-970">0, which means the given directory entry is primary (see [Section 6.3](#63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-971">1, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio dada es secundaria (consulte [la sección 6.4)](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-971">1, which means the given directory entry is secondary (see [Section 6.4](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template))</span></span>

##### <a name="6214-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-972">6.2.1.4 Campo InUse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-972">6.2.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-973">El campo InUse debe describir si la entrada de directorio determinada está en uso o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-973">The InUse field shall describe whether the given directory entry in use or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-974">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-974">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-975">0, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio determinada no está en uso; esto significa que la estructura dada es realmente una entrada de directorio sin usar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-975">0, which means the given directory entry is not in use; this means the given structure actually is an unused directory entry</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-976">1, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio determinada está en uso; esto significa que la estructura dada es una entrada de directorio normal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-976">1, which means the given directory entry is in use; this means the given structure is a regular directory entry</span></span>

#### <a name="622-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-977">6.2.2 Campo FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-977">6.2.2 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-978">El campo FirstCluster debe contener el índice del primer clúster de una asignación en el montón de clúster asociado a la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-978">The FirstCluster field shall contain the index of the first cluster of an allocation in the Cluster Heap associated with the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-979">El intervalo válido de valores para este campo debe ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-979">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-980">Exactamente 0, lo que significa que no existe ninguna asignación de clúster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-980">Exactly 0, which means no cluster allocation exists</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-981">Entre 2 y ClusterCount + 1, que es el intervalo de índices de clúster válidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-981">Between 2 and ClusterCount + 1, which is the range of valid cluster indices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-982">Las estructuras que derivan de esta plantilla pueden volver a definir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength, si una asignación de clúster no es compatible con la estructura derivada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-982">Structures which derive from this template may redefine both the FirstCluster and DataLength fields, if a cluster allocation is not compatible with the derivative structure.</span></span>

#### <a name="623-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-983">6.2.3 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-983">6.2.3 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-984">El campo DataLength describe el tamaño, en bytes, de los datos que contiene la asignación de clúster asociada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-984">The DataLength field describes the size, in bytes, of the data the associated cluster allocation contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-985">El intervalo de valor válido para este campo es:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-985">The valid range of value for this field is:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-986">Al menos 0; si el campo FirstCluster contiene el valor 0, el único valor válido de este campo es 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-986">At least 0; if the FirstCluster field contains the value 0, then this field's only valid value is 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-987">Como máximo ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup> \* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-987">At most ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>\* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-988">Las estructuras que derivan de esta plantilla pueden redefinir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength, si no es posible una asignación de clúster para la estructura derivada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-988">Structures which derive from this template may redefine both the FirstCluster and DataLength fields, if a cluster allocation is not possible for the derivative structure.</span></span>

### <a name="63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-989">6.3 Directorio principal genérico TemplateEntry</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-989">6.3 Generic Primary DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-990">La primera entrada de directorio de un conjunto de entradas de directorio debe ser una entrada de directorio principal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-990">The first directory entry in a directory entry set shall be a primary directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-991">Todas las entradas de directorio subsiguientes, si las hay, en el conjunto de entradas de directorio deben ser entradas de directorio secundario (consulte [la sección 6.4).](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-991">All subsequent directory entries, if any, in the directory entry set shall be secondary directory entries (see [Section 6.4](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-992">La capacidad de interpretar la plantilla Generic Primary DirectoryEntry es obligatoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-992">The ability to interpret the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-993">Todas las estructuras de entrada del directorio principal derivan de la plantilla Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (consulte la tabla [16),](#table-16-generic-primary-directoryentry-template)que deriva de la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (vea [la sección 6.2).](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-993">All primary directory entry structures derive from the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Table 16](#table-16-generic-primary-directoryentry-template)), which derives from the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

#### <a name="631-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1029">6.3.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1029">6.3.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1030">El campo EntryType se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1).](#621-entrytype-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1030">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1](#621-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6311-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1031">6.3.1.1 Campo TypeCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1031">6.3.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1032">El campo TypeCode se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1.1).](#6211-typecode-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1032">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.1](#6211-typecode-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6312-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1033">6.3.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1033">6.3.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1034">El campo TypeImportance se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1.2).](#6212-typeimportance-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1034">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

###### <a name="63121-critical-primary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1035">6.3.1.2.1 Entradas críticas del directorio principal</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1035">6.3.1.2.1 Critical Primary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1036">Las entradas críticas del directorio principal contienen información que es fundamental para la administración adecuada de un volumen ex RAID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1036">Critical primary directory entries contain information which is critical to the proper management of an exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1037">Solo el directorio raíz contiene entradas críticas del directorio principal (las entradas de directorio de archivo son una excepción, vea [la sección 7.4).](#74-file-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1037">Only the root directory contains critical primary directory entries (File directory entries are an exception, see [Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1038">La definición de las entradas críticas del directorio principal se correlaciona con el número de revisión ex LDAP principal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1038">The definition of critical primary directory entries correlates to the major exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1039">Las implementaciones deben admitir todas las entradas críticas del directorio principal y solo registrarán las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que define esta especificación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1039">Implementations shall support all critical primary directory entries and shall only record the critical primary directory entry structures this specification defines.</span></span>

###### <a name="63122-benign-primary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1040">6.3.1.2.2 Entradas de directorio principal benigno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1040">6.3.1.2.2 Benign Primary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1041">Las entradas del directorio principal benigno contienen información adicional que puede ser útil para administrar un volumen ex EX EX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1041">Benign primary directory entries contain additional information which may be useful for managing an exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1042">Cualquier directorio puede contener entradas de directorio principal benignas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1042">Any directory may contain benign primary directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1043">La definición de entradas de directorio principal benignas se correlaciona con el número de revisión ex LDAP menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1043">The definition of benign primary directory entries correlates to the minor exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1044">La compatibilidad con cualquier entrada de directorio principal benigna que defina esta especificación o cualquier especificación posterior es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1044">Support for any benign primary directory entry this specification, or any subsequent specification, defines is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1045">Una entrada de directorio principal benigna no reconocida representa todo el conjunto de entradas de directorio como desconocido (más allá de la definición de las plantillas de entrada de directorio aplicables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1045">An unrecognized benign primary directory entry renders the entire directory entry set as unrecognized (beyond the definition of the applicable directory entry templates).</span></span>

##### <a name="6313-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1046">6.3.1.3 Campo TypeCategory</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1046">6.3.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1047">El campo TypeCategory se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1.3).](#6213-typecategory-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1047">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1048">Para esta plantilla, el valor válido para este campo será 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1048">For this template, the valid value for this field shall be 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="6314-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1049">6.3.1.4 Campo InUse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1049">6.3.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

#### <a name="632-secondarycount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1051">6.3.2 Campo SecondaryCount</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1051">6.3.2 SecondaryCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1052">El campo SecondaryCount describirá el número de entradas de directorio secundario que siguen inmediatamente a la entrada de directorio principal dada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1052">The SecondaryCount field shall describe the number of secondary directory entries which immediately follow the given primary directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1053">Estas entradas de directorio secundario, junto con la entrada de directorio principal dada, componen el conjunto de entradas del directorio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1053">These secondary directory entries, along with the given primary directory entry, comprise the directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1054">El intervalo válido de valores para este campo debe ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1054">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1055">Al menos 0, lo que significa que esta entrada del directorio principal es la única entrada del conjunto de entradas del directorio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1055">At least 0, which means this primary directory entry is the only entry in the directory entry set</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1056">Como máximo 255, lo que significa que las siguientes 255 entradas de directorio y esta entrada del directorio principal componen el conjunto de entradas del directorio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1056">At most 255, which means the next 255 directory entries and this primary directory entry comprise the directory entry set</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1057">Las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que derivan de esta plantilla pueden redefinir los campos SecondaryCount y SetChecksum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1057">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine both the SecondaryCount and SetChecksum fields.</span></span>

#### <a name="633-setchecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1058">6.3.3 Campo SetChecksum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1058">6.3.3 SetChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1059">El campo SetChecksum debe contener la suma de comprobación de todas las entradas de directorio del conjunto de entradas de directorio especificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1059">The SetChecksum field shall contain the checksum of all directory entries in the given directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1060">Sin embargo, la suma de comprobación excluye este campo (vea [la figura 2).](#figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1060">However, the checksum excludes this field (see [Figure 2](#figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1061">Las implementaciones comprobarán que el contenido de este campo es válido antes de usar cualquier otra entrada de directorio en el conjunto de entradas de directorio especificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1061">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using any other directory entry in the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1062">Las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que derivan de esta plantilla pueden redefinir los campos SecondaryCount y SetChecksum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1062">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine both the SecondaryCount and SetChecksum fields.</span></span>

<div id="figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1063">**Figura 2 Cálculo EntrySetChecksum**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1063">**Figure 2 EntrySetChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 EntrySetChecksum
(
    UCHAR * Entries,       // points to an in-memory copy of the directory entry set
    UCHAR   SecondaryCount
)
{
    UInt16 NumberOfBytes = ((UInt16)SecondaryCount + 1) * 32;
    UInt16 Checksum = 0;
    UInt16 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        if ((Index == 2) || (Index == 3))
        {
            continue;
        }
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) +  (UInt16)Entries[Index];
    }
    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="634-generalprimaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1064">6.3.4 Campo GeneralPrimaryFlags</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1064">6.3.4 GeneralPrimaryFlags Field</span></span>

##### <a name="6341-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1086">6.3.4.1 Campo AllocationPossible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1086">6.3.4.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1087">El campo AllocationPossible debe describir si es posible o no una asignación en el montón de clúster para la entrada de directorio determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1087">The AllocationPossible field shall describe whether or not an allocation in the Cluster Heap is possible for the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1088">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1088">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1089">0, lo que significa que no es posible una asignación asociada de clústeres y que los campos FirstCluster y DataLength son realmente indefinidos (las estructuras que derivan de esta plantilla pueden volver a definir esos campos).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1089">0, which means an associated allocation of clusters is not possible and the FirstCluster and DataLength fields are actually undefined (structures which derive from this template may redefine those fields)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1090">1, lo que significa que es posible una asignación asociada de clústeres y que los campos FirstCluster y DataLength están definidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1090">1, which means an associated allocation of clusters is possible and the FirstCluster and DataLength fields are as defined</span></span>

##### <a name="6342-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1091">6.3.4.2 Campo NoCompáin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1091">6.3.4.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1092">El campo NoAturaChain debe indicar si el FAT activo describe o no la cadena de clúster de la asignación dada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1092">The NoFatChain field shall indicate whether or not the active FAT describes the given allocation's cluster chain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1093">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1093">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1094">0, lo que significa que las entradas FAT correspondientes para la cadena de clúster de la asignación son válidas y las implementaciones las interpretarán; si el campo AllocationPossible contiene el valor 0, o si el campo AllocationPossible contiene el valor 1 y el campo FirstCluster contiene el valor 0, el único valor válido de este campo es 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1094">0, which means the corresponding FAT entries for the allocation's cluster chain are valid and implementations shall interpret them; if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0, or if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 1 and the FirstCluster field contains the value 0, then this field's only valid value is 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1095">1, lo que significa que la asignación asociada es una serie contigua de clústeres; las entradas FAT correspondientes para los clústeres no son válidas y las implementaciones no las interpretarán; Las implementaciones pueden usar la ecuación siguiente para calcular el tamaño de la asignación asociada: DataLength/ (2<sup>SectoresPerClusterShift</sup> \* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift)</sup>redondeado al entero más cercano</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1095">1, which means the associated allocation is one contiguous series of clusters; the corresponding FAT entries for the clusters are invalid and implementations shall not interpret them; implementations may use the following equation to calculate the size of the associated allocation: DataLength / (2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>\* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>) rounded up to the nearest integer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1096">Si las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que derivan de esta plantilla redefinen el campo GeneralPrimaryFlags, las entradas FAT correspondientes para cualquier cadena de clúster de asignación asociada son válidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1096">If critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template redefine the GeneralPrimaryFlags field, then the corresponding FAT entries for any associated allocation's cluster chain are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="635-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1097">6.3.5 Campo FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1097">6.3.5 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1098">El campo FirstCluster se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.2).](#622-firstcluster-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1098">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.2](#622-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1099">Si el bit NoApiChain es 1, FirstCluster debe apuntar a un clúster válido en el montón del clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1099">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then FirstCluster must point to a valid cluster in the cluster heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1100">Las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que derivan de esta plantilla pueden redefinir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1100">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1101">Otras estructuras que derivan de esta plantilla pueden volver a definir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength solo si el campo AllocationPossible contiene el valor 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1101">Other structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields only if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="636-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1102">6.3.6 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1102">6.3.6 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1103">El campo DataLength se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.3).](#623-datalength-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1103">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.3](#623-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1104">Si el bit NoImaChain es 1, DataLength no debe ser cero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1104">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then DataLength must not be zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1105">Si el campo FirstCluster es cero, DataLength también debe ser cero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1105">If the FirstCluster field is zero, then DataLength must also be zero.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1106">Las estructuras de entrada de directorio principal críticas que derivan de esta plantilla pueden redefinir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1106">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1107">Otras estructuras que derivan de esta plantilla pueden volver a definir los campos FirstCluster y DataLength solo si el campo AllocationPossible contiene el valor 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1107">Other structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields only if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0.</span></span>

### <a name="64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1108">6.4 Directorio secundario genérico TemplateEntry</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1108">6.4 Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1109">El propósito central de las entradas del directorio secundario es proporcionar información adicional sobre un conjunto de entradas de directorio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1109">The central purpose of secondary directory entries is to provide additional information about a directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1110">La capacidad de interpretar la plantilla Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry es obligatoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1110">The ability to interpret the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1111">La definición de las entradas del directorio secundario crítico e benigno se correlaciona con el número de revisión exLAC menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1111">The definition of both critical and benign secondary directory entries correlates to the minor exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1112">La compatibilidad con cualquier entrada de directorio secundario crítica o benigna que defina esta especificación o especificaciones posteriores es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1112">Support for any critical or benign secondary directory entry this specification, or subsequent specifications, defines is optional.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1113">Todas las estructuras de entrada de directorio secundario derivan de la plantilla Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry (vea la tabla [18),](#table-18-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)que deriva de la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (vea [la sección 6.2).](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1113">All secondary directory entry structures derive from the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Table 18](#table-18-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)), which derives from the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

#### <a name="641-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1141">6.4.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1141">6.4.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

##### <a name="6411-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1143">Campo TypeCode 6.4.1.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1143">6.4.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1144">El campo TypeCode se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1.1).](#6211-typecode-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1144">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.1](#6211-typecode-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6412-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1145">6.4.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1145">6.4.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1146">El campo TypeImportance se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.1.2).](#6212-typeimportance-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1146">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

###### <a name="64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1147">6.4.1.2.1 Entradas críticas de directorio secundario</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1147">6.4.1.2.1 Critical Secondary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1148">Las entradas críticas del directorio secundario contienen información que es fundamental para la administración adecuada de su conjunto de entradas de directorio que lo contiene.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1148">Critical secondary directory entries contain information which is critical to the proper management of its containing directory entry set.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1149">Aunque la compatibilidad con cualquier entrada de directorio secundario crítica específica es opcional, una entrada de directorio crítica no reconocida representa la entrada de directorio completa establecida como no reconocida (más allá de la definición de las plantillas de entrada de directorio aplicables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1149">While support for any specific critical secondary directory entry is optional, an unrecognized critical directory entry renders the entire directory entry set as unrecognized (beyond the definition of the applicable directory entry templates).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1150">Sin embargo, si un conjunto de entradas de directorio contiene al menos una entrada de directorio secundario crítica que una implementación no reconoce, la implementación interpretará como máximo las plantillas de las entradas de directorio en el conjunto de entradas de directorio y no los datos que ninguna asignación asociada a ninguna entrada de directorio del conjunto de entradas de directorio contiene (Las entradas de directorio de archivo son una excepción, vea la sección [7.4).](#74-file-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1150">However, if a directory entry set contains at least one critical secondary directory entry which an implementation does not recognize, then the implementation shall at most interpret the templates of the directory entries in the directory entry set and not the data any allocation associated with any directory entry in the directory entry set contains (File directory entries are an exception, see [Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry)).</span></span>

###### <a name="64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1151">6.4.1.2.2 Entradas de directorio secundario benignas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1151">6.4.1.2.2 Benign Secondary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1152">Las entradas de directorio secundario benignas contienen información adicional que puede ser útil para administrar su conjunto de entradas de directorio que lo contiene.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1152">Benign secondary directory entries contain additional information which may be useful for managing its containing directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1153">La compatibilidad con cualquier entrada de directorio secundario benigna específica es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1153">Support for any specific benign secondary directory entry is optional.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1154">Las entradas de directorio secundario benignas no reconocidas no representan todo el conjunto de entradas de directorio como no reconocidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1154">Unrecognized benign secondary directory entries do not render the entire directory entry set as unrecognized.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1155">Las implementaciones pueden omitir cualquier entrada secundaria benigna que no reconozca.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1155">Implementations may ignore any benign secondary entry it does not recognize.</span></span>

##### <a name="6413-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1156">6.4.1.3 Campo TypeCategory</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1156">6.4.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1158">Para esta plantilla, el valor válido para este campo es 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1158">For this template, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1185">El campo NoCompChain debe tener la misma definición que el campo con el mismo nombre en la plantilla Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (consulte la sección [6.3.4.2).](#6342-nofatchain-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1185">The NoFatChain field shall have the same definition as the same-named field in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.4.2](#6342-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1188">Si el bit NoCompChain es 1, FirstCluster debe apuntar a un clúster válido en el montón del clúster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1188">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then FirstCluster must point to a valid cluster in the cluster heap.</span></span>

#### <a name="644-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1189">6.4.4 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1189">6.4.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1190">El campo DataLength se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.2.3).](#623-datalength-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1190">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.3](#623-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1191">Si el bit NoCompChain es 1, DataLength no debe ser cero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1191">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then DataLength must not be zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1192">Si el campo FirstCluster es cero, DataLength también debe ser cero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1192">If the FirstCluster field is zero, then DataLength must also be zero.</span></span>

## <a name="7-directory-entry-definitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1193">7 Definiciones de entrada de directorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1193">7 Directory Entry Definitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1194">La revisión 1.00 del sistema de archivos ex LDAP define las siguientes entradas de directorio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1194">Revision 1.00 of the exFAT file system defines the following directory entries:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1195">Principal crítica</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1195">Critical primary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1196">Mapa de bits de asignación ([sección 7.1](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1196">Allocation Bitmap ([Section 7.1](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1197">Up-case Table ([Sección 7.2](#72-up-case-table-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1197">Up-case Table ([Section 7.2](#72-up-case-table-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1198">Etiqueta de volumen ([sección 7.3](#73-volume-label-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1198">Volume Label ([Section 7.3](#73-volume-label-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1199">Archivo ([sección 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1199">File ([Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1200">Principal benigna</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1200">Benign primary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1201">GUID de volumen ([sección 7.5](#75-volume-guid-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1201">Volume GUID ([Section 7.5](#75-volume-guid-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1202">Relleno De Texas UNOSI ([Sección 7.10](#710-texfat-padding-directory-entry))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1202">TexFAT Padding ([Section 7.10](#710-texfat-padding-directory-entry))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1203">Secundaria crítica</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1203">Critical secondary</span></span>

### <a name="71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1209">7.1 Entrada de directorio de mapa de bits de asignación</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1209">7.1 Allocation Bitmap Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1210">En el sistema de archivos ex FAT, fat no describe el estado de asignación de los clústeres; en su lugar, lo hace un mapa de bits de asignación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1210">In the exFAT file system, a FAT does not describe the allocation state of clusters; rather, an Allocation Bitmap does.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1211">Los mapas de bits de asignación existen en el montón de clúster (consulte la sección [7.1.5)](#715-allocation-bitmap)y tienen las entradas de directorio principal críticas correspondientes en el directorio raíz (vea la tabla [20).](#table-20-allocation-bitmap-directoryentry-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1211">Allocation Bitmaps exist in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 7.1.5](#715-allocation-bitmap)) and have corresponding critical primary directory entries in the root directory (see [Table 20](#table-20-allocation-bitmap-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1212">El campo NumberOfPlants determina el número de entradas de directorio de mapa de bits de asignación válidas en el directorio raíz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1212">The NumberOfFats field determines the number of valid Allocation Bitmap directory entries in the root directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1213">Si el campo NumberOfPlants contiene el valor 1, el único número válido de entradas del directorio Mapa de bits de asignación es 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1213">If the NumberOfFats field contains the value 1, then the only valid number of Allocation Bitmap directory entries is 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1214">Además, la única entrada del directorio Mapa de bits de asignación solo es válida si describe el primer mapa de bits de asignación (vea la sección [7.1.2.1).](#7121-bitmapidentifier-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1214">Further, the one Allocation Bitmap directory entry is only valid if it describes the First Allocation Bitmap (see [Section 7.1.2.1](#7121-bitmapidentifier-field)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1215">Si el campo NumberOfPlants contiene el valor 2, el único número válido de entradas del directorio Mapa de bits de asignación es 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1215">If the NumberOfFats field contains the value 2, then the only valid number of Allocation Bitmap directory entries is 2.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1216">Además, las dos entradas del directorio Mapa de bits de asignación solo son válidas si una describe el mapa de bits de primera asignación y la otra describe el segundo mapa de bits de asignación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1216">Further, the two Allocation Bitmap directory entries are only valid if one describes the First Allocation Bitmap and the other describes the Second Allocation Bitmap.</span></span>

##### <a name="7121-bitmapidentifier-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1273">7.1.2.1 Campo BitmapIdentifier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1273">7.1.2.1 BitmapIdentifier Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1274">El campo BitmapIdentifier debe indicar qué mapa de bits de asignación describe la entrada de directorio dada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1274">The BitmapIdentifier field shall indicate which Allocation Bitmap the given directory entry describes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1275">Las implementaciones deben usar el primer mapa de bits de asignación junto con la primera FAT y usarán el segundo mapa de bits de asignación junto con el segundo FAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1275">Implementations shall use the First Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the First FAT and shall use the Second Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the Second FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1276">El campo ActiveAtura describe qué FAT y Mapa de bits de asignación están activos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1276">The ActiveFat field describes which FAT and Allocation Bitmap are active.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1277">Los valores válidos para este campo deben ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1277">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1278">0, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio dada describe el primer mapa de bits de asignación</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1278">0, which means the given directory entry describes the First Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1279">1, lo que significa que la entrada de directorio dada describe el segundo mapa de bits de asignación y solo es posible cuando NumberOfPlants contiene el valor 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1279">1, which means the given directory entry describes the Second Allocation Bitmap and is possible only when NumberOfFats contains the value 2</span></span>

#### <a name="713-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1280">7.1.3 FirstCluster Field</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1280">7.1.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1281">El campo FirstCluster se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.3.5).](#635-firstcluster-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1281">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1282">Este campo contiene el índice del primer clúster de la cadena de clúster, como describe FAT, que hospeda el mapa de bits de asignación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1282">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Allocation Bitmap.</span></span>

#### <a name="714-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1283">7.1.4 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1283">7.1.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1284">El campo DataCluster se ajustará a la definición proporcionada en la plantilla Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (consulte [la sección 6.3.6).](#636-datalength-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1284">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="715-allocation-bitmap"></a><span data-ttu-id="a54af-1285">7.1.5 Mapa de bits de asignación</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1285">7.1.5 Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1286">Un mapa de bits de asignación registra el estado de asignación de los clústeres en el montón de clústeres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1286">An Allocation Bitmap records the allocation state of the clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1287">Cada bit de un mapa de bits de asignación indica si su clúster correspondiente está disponible para la asignación o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1287">Each bit in an Allocation Bitmap indicates whether its corresponding cluster is available for allocation or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1288">Un mapa de bits de asignación representa los clústeres del índice más bajo al más alto (consulte [la tabla 22).](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1288">An Allocation Bitmap represents clusters from lowest to highest index (see [Table 22](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a54af-1289">Por motivos históricos, el primer clúster tiene el índice 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1289">For historical reasons, the first cluster has index 2.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a54af-1290">Nota: el primer bit del mapa de bits es el bit de orden más bajo del primer byte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a54af-1290">Note: the first bit in the bitmap is the lowest-order bit of the first byte.</span></span>
